class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Orpheus is a paper sculpture / installation made from 350+ cuts of paper created by <a href=\"https://www.bside.lt/projects/orpheus/\">Aivaras Ligeika</a>. Custom-made glass showcase has a light installed in the base that gently illuminates the sculpture at night-time, creating a unique experience for the observer.</p>\n\n<p>The author explores the relationship between a human and matter, and realizes the desire to form the environment reflecting the image of a thought. Hundreds of illusions cut from sheets of paper create a harmonious, sculptural object reminiscent of a mute symphony of dreams and ideas. The unsustainable matter embodies the fragility of the moment of the life of thought.</p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/551337430\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1320px;margin:auto;\">\n<div style=\"left: 0; about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>05.18.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p> </p>\n\n<p><meta charset=\"utf-8\" /></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/DM2graphics\">Mario De Meyer</a> shared a set of really intriguing vector illustrations titled Novelty Waves. It’s the fourth installment of the series where Mario explores organic ways to deform lines. Imagine a 3D topographic view on steroids. The most fascinating thing is the tool of choice for this work. Mario mentions Illustrator alone, which makes me wonder how he did them. My first guess was that it was done using Photoshop Displace Map or even 3D. It looks like we will have to wait for a future tutorial or walkthrough from the designer. Meanwhile, check them out and let us know what you think.</p>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\">Vector Illustration</h2>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\" dir=\"ltr\"><img           <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/oin-ye-exhibiton-branding-recognize-asian-culture\"><img to recognize the Asian culture\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>05.17.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Oin Ye is a ceramic artist from Vietnam. He is more known regionally and sells selected products at exhibitions or art markets. For Oin Ye next exhibition \"Collection 2\" <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/fabiobiesel\">Studio Fabio Biesel</a> were allowed to develop the branding and visual identity work.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/fabiobiesel\">Studio Fabio Biesel</a> created print and editorial products like posters, a catalog, cards, etc. The result is really impressive and very personal.</p>\n\n<p><q class=\"pullquote\">We want the brand to recognize the Asian culture. — Studio Fabio Biesel</q></p>\n\n<p>Basic Idea: It's all about culture. From the beginning the designers were looking for something very cultural and personal. They found the sketches and the artist's handwriting very strong and memorable. So they used these as the basis for the entire identity. </p>\n\n<h3 class=\"imgsGrid\">Branding</h3>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img alt=\"artist,brand,clean,Corporate xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>05.16.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/plasticbionic\">Plasticbionic .</a>, <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/etiennemurphy\">Etienne Murphy</a> and <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/scgvr\">Simon Chénier-Gauvreau</a> shared a branding and visual identity project for SCALE AI which the objective is to accelerate the application of artificial intelligence for supply chains. The designers created the scale. Both logo and graphic device, it helps them highlight the values, connect different ideas, and create original and malleable grids for various touchpoints. Above all, the scale illustrates SCALE AI vision to develop a thriving AI ecosystem, scaling businesses along the way.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"3D,ai,branding
